<script>
function changePhoneNumber(){ 
    /* promo stiicky updates */
    try {
    var e = document.querySelectorAll("div[class='pzn-container']")[0];
    var parentElem =e.parentElement;

          if(document.querySelector("#desktopPromoView")){
            if(parentElem){
              parentElem.style.top='80px'; 
              parentElem.style.height='80px'; 
              parentElem.style.zIndex='9999'; 
              parentElem.style.position='sticky'; 
            }
            
          }else{
            if(parentElem){
              parentElem.style.top='0px';
              parentElem.style.height='80px'; 
              parentElem.style.zIndex='9999'; 
              parentElem.style.position='sticky';   
            }
          }

    } catch (err) {
            console.log(err.message);
    }
  
}

document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(e){
  try {
         changePhoneNumber();
           const targetNodes = document.querySelectorAll('body');
           targetNodes.forEach(function(targetNode){
               const config = { attributes: true, childList: true, subtree: true }
               const observer = new MutationObserver(function(){
                   observer.disconnect()
                   changePhoneNumber();
                   observer.observe(targetNode, config)
               })
               observer.observe(targetNode, config)
           })
   } catch (e) {
       console.log(e);
   }
});


/* Decibels */
(function() {
    function onDecibelReady() {
    decibelInsight(
        'sendIntegrationData',
        'GenericIntegration',
        {
            id: '74d04940-75ae-11ed-921e-813b73c10a7d',
            name: 'SBSEGQBMCRGutenbergQbks31398GlobalnavLive'
        }
    );
    }
    if (window.hasOwnProperty('decibelInsight')) {
        decibelInsight('ready', onDecibelReady);
    } else {
        window['_da_ready'] = onDecibelReady;
    }
})();
</script></div></div></div></div><div><div data-testid="Codeblock" class="root"><div class="innerhtml"><script>

QuickBooks offer bookkeeping services?" data-object="content" data-ui-object="accordion_item_1" data-sku="" data-action="interacted" data-ui-action="displayed" pricingContext="[object Object]" index="0"><div style="color:#000000;font-size:">Does QuickBooks offer bookkeeping services?</div><div class="AccordionItem_blackArrow__f0c42aa7"></div></button><div id="panel-87434d3c-df10-4dcd-aa54-18e44438970b-0" aria-labelledby="accordion-87434d3c-df10-4dcd-aa54-18e44438970b-0" role="region" class="AccordionItem_itemPanel__f0c42aa7"><div data-testid="animHeight" style="height:0;overflow:hidden" aria-hidden="true" class="rah-static rah-static--height-zero"><div style="transition:opacity 417ms ease 0ms;-webkit-transition:opacity 417ms ease 0ms;opacity:0"><div class="AccordionItem_content__f0c42aa7"><div data-testid="Responsivetext" class="Responsivetext_responsivetext__3adcf43c Responsivetext_blackColor__3adcf43c" style="max-width:800px"><div class="text"><div class='resp-text-wrapper'><p>Yes! QuickBooks Live Bookkeeping is an online bookkeeping service that connects small businesses with trusted, QuickBooks-certified virtual bookkeepers. Your bookkeeper takes the lead on your bookkeeping and runs essential reports so you can focus on your business.</p><p><br></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="AccordionItem_itemContainer__f0c42aa7"><div class="item" data-testid="accordionItem" data-tracking="accordion_item_2" data-ax-id=""><button class="AccordionItem_toggle__f0c42aa7" class="AccordionItem_blackArrow__f0c42aa7"></div></button><div id="panel-f6419914-23e0-460e-81c8-c87a080dd1f0-1" aria-labelledby="accordion-f6419914-23e0-460e-81c8-c87a080dd1f0-1" role="region" class="AccordionItem_itemPanel__f0c42aa7"><div data-testid="animHeight" style="height:0;overflow:hidden" aria-hidden="true" class="rah-static rah-static--height-zero"><div style="transition:opacity Responsivetext_blackColor__3adcf43c"><div class="text"><div class='resp-text-wrapper'><p>Typical cleanup is complete within 30 days after receiving all necessary documentation.</p><p><br></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="AccordionItem_itemContainer__f0c42aa7"><div class="item" data-testid="accordionItem" data-tracking="accordion_item_3" data-ax-id=""><button class="AccordionItem_toggle__f0c42aa7" data-testid="accItemButton" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="panel-89245ecf-b814-4963-9682-eaa7ef1fe93c-2" id="accordion-89245ecf-b814-4963-9682-eaa7ef1fe93c-2" tabindex="0" data-ui-access-point="" data-wa-link="faq-3" data-ui-object-detail="What’s included in QuickBooks Live Full-Service Bookkeeping?" data-object="content" data-ui-object="accordion_item_3" data-sku="" data-action="interacted" data-ui-action="displayed" pricingContext="[object Object]" index="0"><div style="color:#000000;font-size:">What’s included in QuickBooks Live Full-Service Bookkeeping?</div><div class="AccordionItem_blackArrow__f0c42aa7"></div></button><div id="panel-89245ecf-b814-4963-9682-eaa7ef1fe93c-2" aria-labelledby="accordion-89245ecf-b814-4963-9682-eaa7ef1fe93c-2" role="region" class="AccordionItem_itemPanel__f0c42aa7"><div data-testid="animHeight" style="height:0;overflow:hidden" aria-hidden="true" class="rah-static rah-static--height-zero"><div style="transition:opacity 417ms ease 0ms;-webkit-transition:opacity 417ms ease 0ms;opacity:0"><div class="AccordionItem_content__f0c42aa7"><div data-testid="Responsivetext" class="Responsivetext_responsivetext__3adcf43c Responsivetext_blackColor__3adcf43c"><div class="text"><div class='resp-text-wrapper'><p class="ql-align-justify">Full-Service Bookkeeping includes two phases: cleanup and ongoing bookkeeping</p><ul><li>In the cleanup/setup phase, your bookkeeper helps you set up your chart of accounts, connects your banks, and teaches you the basics of QuickBooks. If you have information in QuickBooks already, your bookkeeper will help clean it up in the first month of service.</li><li>As part of ongoing bookkeeping, your bookkeeper categorizes your transactions and reconciles your accounts each month.</li><li class="ql-align-justify">Your bookkeeper can close your books and prepare a trial balance. They can also send PDF copies of key financial reports including your profit and loss statement and balance sheet.</li></ul><p class="ql-align-justify"><br></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="AccordionItem_itemContainer__f0c42aa7"><div class="item" data-testid="accordionItem" data-tracking="accordion_item_4" data-ax-id=""><button class="AccordionItem_toggle__f0c42aa7" data-testid="accItemButton" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="panel-e8a6a4ef-c838-46b7-96a2-d0339e7482cb-3" id="accordion-e8a6a4ef-c838-46b7-96a2-d0339e7482cb-3" tabindex="0" data-ui-access-point="" data-wa-link="faq-4" data-ui-object-detail="What’s not included in QuickBooks Live Full-Service Bookkeeping?" data-object="content" data-ui-object="accordion_item_4" data-sku="" data-action="interacted" data-ui-action="displayed" pricingContext="[object Object]" index="0"><div style="color:#000000;font-size:">What’s not included in QuickBooks Live Full-Service Bookkeeping?</div><div class="AccordionItem_blackArrow__f0c42aa7"></div></button><div id="panel-e8a6a4ef-c838-46b7-96a2-d0339e7482cb-3" aria-labelledby="accordion-e8a6a4ef-c838-46b7-96a2-d0339e7482cb-3" role="region" class="AccordionItem_itemPanel__f0c42aa7"><div data-testid="animHeight" style="height:0;overflow:hidden" aria-hidden="true" class="rah-static rah-static--height-zero"><div style="transition:opacity 417ms ease 0ms;-webkit-transition:opacity 417ms ease 0ms;opacity:0"><div class="AccordionItem_content__f0c42aa7"><div data-testid="Responsivetext" class="Responsivetext_responsivetext__3adcf43c Responsivetext_blackColor__3adcf43c"><div class="text"><div class='resp-text-wrapper'><p>Full-Service Bookkeeping doesn’t include sending invoices, paying bills, or management of inventory, accounts receivable, or accounts payable. The service doesn’t include financial advisory services, tax advice, facilitating the filing of income or sales tax returns, creating or sending 1099s, or management of payroll. QuickBooks Online offers Full Service Payroll for an <a href="https://quickbooks.intuit.com/payroll/pricing/" data-wa-link="faq-4-cost" data-action="interacted" data-object="content" data-ui-action="clicked" data-ui-object="link" data-ui-object-detail="additional cost." data-ui-access-point="" data-sku="" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-object-detail="">additional cost</a>.</p><p><br></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="AccordionItem_itemContainer__f0c42aa7"><div class="item" data-testid="accordionItem" data-tracking="accordion_item_5" data-ax-id=""><button class="AccordionItem_toggle__f0c42aa7" data-testid="accItemButton" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="panel-524cded1-4c03-4fbc-a4a3-d0ff9ecbb98c-4" id="accordion-524cded1-4c03-4fbc-a4a3-d0ff9ecbb98c-4" tabindex="0" data-ui-access-point="" data-wa-link="faq-5" data-ui-object-detail="I already have QuickBooks Online. Can I buy Live Bookkeeping?" data-object="content" data-ui-object="accordion_item_5" data-sku="" data-action="interacted" data-ui-action="displayed" pricingContext="[object Object]" index="0"><div style="color:#000000;font-size:">I already have QuickBooks Online. Can I buy Live Bookkeeping?</div><div class="AccordionItem_blackArrow__f0c42aa7"></div></button><div id="panel-524cded1-4c03-4fbc-a4a3-d0ff9ecbb98c-4" aria-labelledby="accordion-524cded1-4c03-4fbc-a4a3-d0ff9ecbb98c-4" role="region" class="AccordionItem_itemPanel__f0c42aa7"><div data-testid="animHeight" style="height:0;overflow:hidden" aria-hidden="true" class="rah-static rah-static--height-zero"><div style="transition:opacity 417ms ease 0ms;-webkit-transition:opacity 417ms ease 0ms;opacity:0"><div class="AccordionItem_content__f0c42aa7"><div data-testid="Responsivetext" class="Responsivetext_responsivetext__3adcf43c grey"><div class="text"><div class='resp-text-wrapper'><p>Yes! You can subscribe to QuickBooks Live Bookkeeping by <a href="https://c1.qbo.intuit.com/qbo1/login?pagereq=livebookkeeping" data-wa-link="faq-5-signin" data-action="interacted" data-object="content" data-ui-action="clicked" data-ui-object="link" data-ui-object-detail="signing in to your QuickBooks Online account or by calling sales. For pricing and subscription details, see Important pricing details and product information below.</p><p><br></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="AccordionItem_itemContainer__f0c42aa7"><div class="item" data-testid="accordionItem" data-tracking="accordion_item_6" data-ax-id=""><button class="AccordionItem_toggle__f0c42aa7" data-testid="accItemButton" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="panel-d6b3d698-f09a-486c-b306-29ae72e7417b-5" id="accordion-d6b3d698-f09a-486c-b306-29ae72e7417b-5" tabindex="0" data-ui-access-point="" data-wa-link="faq-6" data-ui-object-detail="How much time do I get with my bookkeeper each month?" data-object="content" data-ui-object="accordion_item_6" data-sku="" data-action="interacted" data-ui-action="displayed" pricingContext="[object Object]" index="0"><div style="color:#000000;font-size:">How much time do I get with my bookkeeper each month?</div><div class="AccordionItem_blackArrow__f0c42aa7"></div></button><div id="panel-d6b3d698-f09a-486c-b306-29ae72e7417b-5" aria-labelledby="accordion-d6b3d698-f09a-486c-b306-29ae72e7417b-5" role="region" class="AccordionItem_itemPanel__f0c42aa7"><div data-testid="animHeight" style="height:0;overflow:hidden" aria-hidden="true" class="rah-static rah-static--height-zero"><div style="transition:opacity 417ms ease 0ms;-webkit-transition:opacity 417ms ease 0ms;opacity:0"><div class="AccordionItem_content__f0c42aa7"><div data-testid="Responsivetext" class="Responsivetext_responsivetext__3adcf43c Responsivetext_blackColor__3adcf43c"><div class="text"><div class='resp-text-wrapper'><p>There’s no set amount of time you get per month. Small businesses often schedule video appointments once or twice per month to discuss questions and to review results. You’re limited to one scheduled appointment at a time and appointments have to work within your bookkeeper’s schedule. Communications that are available any time include document sharing and live chat with a member of your bookkeeper’s extended team.</p><p><br></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="AccordionItem_itemContainer__f0c42aa7"><div class="item" data-testid="accordionItem" data-tracking="accordion_item_7" data-ax-id=""><button class="AccordionItem_toggle__f0c42aa7" data-testid="accItemButton" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="panel-06634356-f4f4-4557-9370-b048bce929c1-6" id="accordion-06634356-f4f4-4557-9370-b048bce929c1-6" tabindex="0" data-ui-access-point="" data-wa-link="faq-7" data-ui-object-detail="Can I switch plans or cancel at any time?" data-object="content" data-ui-object="accordion_item_7" data-sku="" data-action="interacted" data-ui-action="displayed" pricingContext="[object Object]" index="0"><div style="color:#000000;font-size:">Can I switch plans or cancel at any time?</div><div class="AccordionItem_blackArrow__f0c42aa7"></div></button><div id="panel-06634356-f4f4-4557-9370-b048bce929c1-6" aria-labelledby="accordion-06634356-f4f4-4557-9370-b048bce929c1-6" role="region" class="AccordionItem_itemPanel__f0c42aa7"><div data-testid="animHeight" style="height:0;overflow:hidden" aria-hidden="true" class="rah-static rah-static--height-zero"><div style="transition:opacity 417ms ease 0ms;-webkit-transition:opacity 417ms ease 0ms;opacity:0"><div class="AccordionItem_content__f0c42aa7"><div data-testid="Responsivetext" class="Responsivetext_responsivetext__3adcf43c Responsivetext_blackColor__3adcf43c"><div class="text"><div class='resp-text-wrapper'><p>Yes, you’re free to switch QuickBooks Online plans or cancel at any time. QuickBooks Live customers may cancel plans at any time.</p><p><br></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div><div data-testid="Fragment" data-tracking="fragment"><div><!-- Live Chat - Reimagined - HTML Start -->

<script>
  var chatBox = document.getElementsByClassName('chat--box')[0];
  var chatContainer = document.getElementsByClassName('chat--container')[0];
  var closeButton = document.querySelectorAll(".chat--box .close--button")[0];
  var scheduleCallElem = document.querySelectorAll(".schedule-call-link")[0];
  var scheduleCallClose = document.querySelectorAll(".schedule-close")[0];
  var scheduleContainer = document.getElementsByClassName("schedule-section")[0];
  var scheduleIframe = document.getElementById("schedulCallIframe");
  var scheduleModal = document.getElementsByClassName("chat--phone");
  var  lpSectionDesktop = 'livereimagine:qbl-reimagine-button-div';
  var scheduleCallLink = "https://intuit.chilipiper.com/book/variant-qblive-magic-carpet-main-page";
  var modalPhoneNumber = "1-800-315-1484";
  if(chatContainer != undefined){
  chatContainer.addEventListener("click",function(){
     chatBox.style.display = "block";
     chatContainer.style.display = "none";
  });
  }
  if(closeButton!= undefined){
     closeButton.addEventListener("click", function(){
         chatBox.style.display = "none";
         chatContainer.style.display = "block";
     });
  }
  if(scheduleCallElem != undefined){
    /* scheduleCallElem.addEventListener("click",function(){
        scheduleIframe.setAttribute("src",scheduleCallLink);

         chatBox.style.display = "none";
         scheduleContainer.style.display = "block";
    });*/
     }
     if(scheduleCallClose != undefined){
         scheduleCallClose.addEventListener("click",function(){
            chatBox.style.display = "block";
            scheduleContainer.style.display = "none";
        });
         }
         scheduleModal.innerHTML = modalPhoneNumber;
</script>
<!-- Live Chat - Reimagined - JS End -->
<script>
/* proactive chat blocking solution*/
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(e){
        try {
            
            /* Targeting Blocks that will have state change & HTML re-rendered */
            const targetNodes = document.querySelectorAll('body');
            targetNodes.forEach(function(targetNode){
                /* Options for the observer (which mutations to observe) */
                const config = { attributes: true, childList: true, subtree: true }
                /* Create an observer instance linked to the callback function */
                const observer = new MutationObserver(function(mutationsList, observer){
                    var executeMethod = false;
                    /* To avoid infinite loop, disconnect the observer first */
                    observer.disconnect();
                    mutationsList.forEach(function(mutation){
                        if (mutation.target.classList.contains('lp_desktop')) {
                            executeMethod = true;
                        }
                        if (mutation.target.classList.contains('LPMoverlay') && document.body.childNodes[0].classList.contains('LPMoverlay')) {
                            console.log('Chat Updates: Proactive Chat window displayed, Time :',Date());
                        }
                    });
                    if (executeMethod) {
                        document.body.classList.add('chat-initiated');
                        console.log('Chat Updates: Chat initiated by visitor');
                    }
                    /* Start observing the target node again */
                    observer.observe(targetNode, config);
                })
                /* Start observing the target node for configured mutations */
                observer.observe(targetNode, config);
            });
            var chatContainer = document.getElementsByClassName('chat--container')[0];
            var closeButton = document.querySelectorAll(".chat--box .close--button")[0];
            if(chatContainer != undefined){
                chatContainer.addEventListener("click",function(){
                    document.body.classList.add('chat-box-displayed');
                });
            }
            if(closeButton!= undefined){
                closeButton.addEventListener("click", function(){
                    setTimeout(function(){
                        document.body.classList.remove('chat-box-displayed');
                    },30000);
                });
            }
            document.addEventListener("click",function(event){
                console.log(event.target.matches('[data-wa-link="sales_widget_chat"]'))
                console.log(event.target.matches('[data-lp-point="confirm_button"]'))
          
                if (event.target.matches('[data-wa-link="sales_widget_chat"]')) {
                    chatBox.style.display = "none";
                    //chatContainer.style.display = "block";
                } else if (event.target.matches('[data-lp-point="confirm_button"]')) {
                    if (chatContainer && window.getComputedStyle(chatContainer).getPropertyValue('display') === "none") {
                        chatBox.style.display = "block";
                    }
                }
            });
        } catch(e) {
            console.error(e)
        }
    });
</script>

and up to date all year when you partner with a Live Bookkeeper.</p></div></div><div class="RwBanner_rwCtaParentContainer__69a9eb3f"><div class="align-left"><button data-testid="button" data-tracking="button" class="Button_button__2a83db50 Button_rwLarge__2a83db50 Button_rwPrimary__2a83db50 RwBanner_rwCta__69a9eb3f align-left" aria-label="" href="" data-targetmodalid="disclaimermodal" title="" data-ui-access-point="" data-wa-link="close-consult-cta" data-ui-object-detail="Get a free consultation" data-object="content" data-ui-object="button" data-sku="" data-action="interacted" data-ui-action="clicked" blockName="qbmds/button"><span class="Button_buttonText__2a83db50">Get a free consultation</span></button></div></div></div></div></div><div><div data-testid="RwDisclaimer" data-tracking="disclaimer" class="RwDisclaimer_rwDisclaimer__b177b25c RwDisclaimer_fullWidth__b177b25c"><div class="RwDisclaimer_rwDisclaimer__container__b177b25c" style="background-color:#0fd46c"><div class="RwDisclaimer_rwDisclaimer__linkContainer__b177b25c"><button class="Link_link__829fb056 RwDisclaimer_rwDisclaimer__link__b177b25c Link_rwDarkBlue__829fb056 Link_body02__829fb056 Link_medium__829fb056" data-testid="link" data-tracking="link" title="" rel="" aria-expanded="false" data-ui-access-point="" data-wa-link="close-disc" data-ui-object-detail="Important pricing details and product information" data-object="content" data-ui-object="link" data-sku="" data-action="interacted" data-ui-action=""><span>Important pricing details and product information<span class="RwDisclaimer_rwDisclaimer__icon__b177b25c"><svg width="17" height="8" viewBox="0 0 17 8" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M1 0.875L6.45305 5.96451C7.60567 7.04029 9.39433 7.04029 10.547 5.96451L16 0.875" stroke="#0D333F" stroke-width="2"></path></svg></span></span></button></div><div class="rah-static rah-static--height-zero RwDisclaimer_rwDisclaimer__accordionWrapper__b177b25c RwDisclaimer_contentBackgroundWhite__b177b25c" style="height:0;overflow:hidden" aria-hidden="true"><div style="transition:opacity 400ms ease 250ms;-webkit-transition:opacity 400ms ease 250ms;opacity:0"><div class="RwDisclaimer_rwDisclaimer__content__b177b25c"><div data-testid="RwDisclaimerGroup" data-tracking="rw_disclaimer_group" class="RwDisclaimerGroup_rwDisclaimerGroup__a0509c66 RwDisclaimerGroup_darkTheme__a0509c66"><div class="rw-disclaimer-group__header"><div data-testid="Responsivetext" class="Responsivetext_responsivetext__3adcf43c RwDisclaimerGroup_rwDisclaimerGroup__subhead__a0509c66 Responsivetext_blackColor__3adcf43c"><div class="text"><div class='resp-text-wrapper'><p><strong>Guarantees</strong></p><p><strong>Accurate Books Guarantee</strong>: At your request, QuickBooks will conduct a full evaluation of your bookkeeper’s work. If your Live Bookkeeper makes an error that requires you to re-open your books for any month, we’ll correct the error in your books for the month that the error occurred at no additional charge.</p><p>Eligible errors include only those made by a Live Bookkeeper. An “error” is: a) a transaction that has been incorrectly categorized to the wrong account; b) an account balance in QuickBooks that doesn’t match the actual account balance; or c) improper transactions which can’t be supported by documentation (including client responses and client meeting notes).</p><p>If you invoke the guarantee, QuickBooks will conduct an evaluation of the Live Bookkeeper’s work. You’ll need to provide QuickBooks with a receipt for the transaction in question, correspondence from your outside tax accountant, or a document stating the balance of the account if an account balance is in question.</p><p>Live Bookkeepers aren’t responsible for errors resulting from incorrect information that you provide, or if you re-open the books by overriding closure after a Live Bookkeeper completes the month-end closure.</p><p><br></p><p><strong>**Product information</strong></p><p><strong>QuickBooks Live Monthly Bookkeeping pricing tiers</strong>: Live Bookkeeping is available to QuickBooks Online subscribers and is sold separately. QuickBooks Live Cleanup is required for Live Monthly Bookkeeping. Cleanup fee is customized based on signup month, tax filing status, and business start date. Following a 30 day period after signup, the ongoing Live Bookkeeping service is available in 3 different pricing tiers, depending on your company’s average monthly expenses over a period of 3 consecutive months. After the first month, you’ll be charged monthly at the then-current monthly fee based on your average monthly expenses over the previous 3 months, unless you cancel. Your business’s average monthly expenses and associated subscription pricing may be reassessed at Intuit’s sole discretion. Currently:</p><ul><li><span style="background-color: transparent;">If your monthly average is $0-10,000 per month, the monthly price for QuickBooks Live is $200. </span></li><li><span style="background-color: transparent;">If your monthly average is $10,001-50,000, the monthly price for QuickBooks Live is $300. </span></li><li><span style="background-color: transparent;">If your monthly average is $50,001 or more, the monthly price for QuickBooks Live is $400.</span></li></ul><p><br></p><p><strong>QuickBook Live Monthly Bookkeeping services</strong>: After signup, a Live Bookkeeper provides cleanup services that start from the date of your last business tax return or business incorporation date (if more recent) through the end of the calendar month before first sign-up to Live Bookkeeping. The services provided during the first month are as follows, as applicable: update bookkeeping based on information you provide; connect bank and credit cards; categorize and update transactions up until the last tax-filing date; reconcile bank and credit card accounts with past statements, as provided by you; reconcile remaining balance sheet accounts; and run a summary report of work completed, balance sheet, and profit loss statement of YTD for cleanup period(s).</p><p>A Live Bookkeeper cannot begin cleaning up your past books until they receive the required supporting documentation, which your bookkeeper will request from you after your first meeting. Once your bookkeeper receives all the necessary documentation, they’ll typically complete your cleanup within 30 days. In some cases, your cleanup may take longer depending on timeliness of documentation and the complexity of your books.</p><p>During each subsequent month, ongoing Live Bookkeeping services include: an overview of the main features of QBO; setup of customers and vendors; assistance with reports and reporting tools; setup of chart of accounts; assistance with bank connections, expense type classification, categorization, and reconciliation based on information you provide; importing of historical data; and ongoing assistance with bookkeeping practices). Some basic bookkeeping services may not be included and will be determined by your Live Bookkeeper. The Live Bookkeeper will provide help based on the information you provide. For more information about services provided by Live Bookkeeping, refer to the <a href="https://glam.app.intuit.com/app/guesttos?glocale=en_US" data-wa-link="disc-qb-tos" data-action="interacted" data-object="content" data-ui-action="clicked" data-ui-object="link" data-ui-object-detail="QuickBooks Terms of Service. " data-ui-access-point="" data-sku="" rel="noopener noreferrer" data-object-detail="">QuickBooks Terms of Service</a>. </p><p><br></p><p><strong>QuickBooks Live Bookkeeping Cleanup</strong>: The QuickBooks Live Bookkeeping Cleanup only applies to bookkeeping records up to your last tax filing. You must have filed your business’ prior tax return and provide a copy of the return before cleanup services can begin. A Live Bookkeeper cannot begin cleaning up your past books until they receive all of the required supporting documentation, which your bookkeeper will request from you after your first meeting. Once your bookkeeper receives all the necessary documentation, they’ll typically complete your cleanup within 30 days. In some cases, your cleanup may take longer depending on timeliness of documentation and the complexity of your books.</p><p><br></p><p><br></p><p><br></p><p><strong>Tax-ready books:</strong> Live Bookkeeping doesn’t include tax preparation services or assistance with tax preparation, or assurance services. Consult a tax preparer for tax advice related to the preparation of your tax return. The Live Bookkeeping Cleanup service is from the date of your last business tax return through the end of the calendar month before first sign-up to Live Bookkeeping.</p><p><strong>#Claims</strong></p><p><br></p><p><br></p><p><span class="ql-font-medium01 ql-size-regular">1. </span><span class="ql-font-large ql-size-demi">Time savings:</span><span class="ql-font-medium01 ql-size-regular"> Based on a survey of QuickBooks Live Bookkeeping customers, as of November 2021.</span></p><p><br></p><p><span class="ql-font-medium01 ql-size-regular">2. </span><span class="ql-font-large ql-size-demi">Bookkeeper experience:</span><span class="ql-font-medium01 ql-size-regular"> Based on internal data, as of November 2021.</span></p><p><br></p><p><span class="ql-font-medium01 ql-size-regular">3. </span><span class="ql-font-large ql-size-demi">Tax time:</span><span class="ql-font-medium01 ql-size-regular"> Based on a survey of QuickBooks Live Bookkeeping customers, as of November 2021.</span></p><p><br></p><p><span class="ql-font-medium01 ql-size-regular">4. </span><span class="ql-font-large ql-size-demi">Matching:</span><span class="ql-font-medium01 ql-size-regular"> Customers are automatically matched with a Live Bookkeeper that has experience in their relevant industry, unless one is unavailable. After a customer has connected with the assigned bookkeeper, they may request to be matched with a different bookkeeper, if they prefer.</span></p><p><br></p><p><span class="ql-font-medium01 ql-size-regular">5. </span><span class="ql-font-large ql-size-demi">Collaboration:</span><span class="ql-font-medium01 ql-size-regular"> Based on a survey of QuickBooks Live Bookkeeping customers who used QuickBooks Live Bookkeeping for more than 3 months, as of November 2021.</span></p><p><br></p><p><br></p><p>Terms, conditions, pricing, special features, and service and support options subject to change without notice.</p></div></div></div></div><div class="rw-disclaimer-group__content"><div data-testid="RwDisclaimerItem" data-tracking="rw_disclaimer_item"     /* Phone number update */
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(e){
        try {
            if((window.getCustCookie("mds_3rdparty_experience_store") && window.getCustCookie("mds_3rdparty_experience_store").indexOf("45657_110434") > -1) || window.getCustCookie('enablePhoneChanges')){

                /* Decibels */
                (function() {
                    function onDecibelReady() {
                    decibelInsight(
                        'sendIntegrationData',
                        'GenericIntegration',
                        {
                            id: '45657_110434',
                            name: 'QB_QBKS_30114_WB_R_WR_Mobile_Test_Treatment1'

                executeRWTestChangeMethod();
                /* Targeting Blocks that will have state change & HTML re-rendered */
                var targetNodes = document.querySelectorAll('[data-testid="RwGlobalNav"]');
                targetNodes.forEach(function(targetNode){
                    /* Options for the observer (which mutations to observe) */
                    var config = { attributes: true, childList: true, subtree: true }
                    /* Create an observer instance linked to the callback function */
                    var observer = new MutationObserver(function(mutationsList, observer){
                        var executeMethod = false;
                        /* To avoid infinite loop, disconnect the observer first */
                        observer.disconnect();
                        mutationsList.forEach(function(mutation){
                            /*console.log(mutation.target.classList);*/
                            if (mutation.target.classList.value.indexOf('RwGlobalNav') > -1 && (mutation.target.classList.value.indexOf('mobileView') > -1 || mutation.target.classList.value.indexOf('RwGlobalNav_sectionOpen__') > -1)) {
                                executeMethod = true;
                            }
                        });
                        if (executeMethod) {
                            executeRWTestChangeMethod();
                        }
                        /* Start observing the target node again */
                        observer.observe(targetNode, config);
                    })
                    /* Start observing the target node for configured mutations */
                    observer.observe(targetNode, config);
                });
            }
        } catch(e) {
            console.error(e);
        }
    });

class='resp-text-wrapper'\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eGuarantees\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAccurate Books Guarantee\u003c/strong\u003e: At your request, QuickBooks will conduct a full evaluation of your bookkeeper’s work. If your Live Bookkeeper makes an error that requires you to re-open your books for any month, we’ll correct the error in your books for the month that the error occurred at no additional charge.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eEligible errors include only those made by a Live Bookkeeper. An “error” is: a) a transaction that has been incorrectly categorized to the wrong account; b) an account balance in QuickBooks that doesn’t match the actual account balance; or c) improper transactions which can’t be supported by documentation (including client responses and client meeting notes).\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eIf you invoke the guarantee, QuickBooks will conduct an evaluation of the Live Bookkeeper’s work. You’ll need to provide QuickBooks with a receipt for the transaction in question, correspondence from your outside tax accountant, or a document stating the balance of the account if an account balance is in question.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eLive Bookkeepers aren’t responsible for errors resulting from incorrect information that you provide, or if you re-open the books by overriding closure after a Live Bookkeeper completes the month-end closure.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cbr\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e**Product information\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eQuickBooks Live Monthly Bookkeeping pricing tiers\u003c/strong\u003e: Live Bookkeeping is available to QuickBooks Online subscribers and is sold separately. QuickBooks Live Cleanup is required for Live Monthly Bookkeeping. Cleanup fee is customized based on signup month, tax filing status, and business start date. Following a 30 day period after signup, the ongoing Live Bookkeeping service is available in 3 different pricing tiers, depending on your company’s average monthly expenses over a period of 3 consecutive months. After the first month, you’ll be charged monthly at the then-current monthly fee based on your average monthly expenses over the previous 3 months, unless you cancel. Your business’s average monthly expenses and associated subscription pricing may be reassessed at Intuit’s sole discretion. Currently:\u003c/p\u003e\u003cul\u003e\u003cli\u003e\u003cspan style=\"background-color: transparent;\"\u003eIf your monthly average is $0-10,000 per month, the monthly price for QuickBooks Live is $200. \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\u003cli\u003e\u003cspan style=\"background-color: transparent;\"\u003eIf your monthly average is $10,001-50,000, the monthly price for QuickBooks Live is $300. \u003c/span\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\u003cli\u003e\u003cspan style=\"background-color: transparent;\"\u003eIf your monthly average is $50,001 or more, the monthly price for QuickBooks Live is $400.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/li\u003e\u003c/ul\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cbr\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eQuickBook Live Monthly Bookkeeping services\u003c/strong\u003e: After signup, a Live Bookkeeper provides cleanup services that start from the date of your last business tax return or business incorporation date (if more recent) through the end of the calendar month before first sign-up to Live Bookkeeping. The services provided during the first month are as follows, as applicable: update bookkeeping based on information you provide; connect bank and credit cards; categorize and update transactions up until the last tax-filing date; reconcile bank and credit card accounts with past statements, as provided by you; reconcile remaining balance sheet accounts; and run a summary report of work completed, balance sheet, and profit loss statement of YTD for cleanup period(s).\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eA Live Bookkeeper cannot begin cleaning up your past books until they receive the required supporting documentation, which your bookkeeper will request from you after your first meeting. Once your bookkeeper receives all the necessary documentation, they’ll typically complete your cleanup within 30 days. In some cases, your cleanup may take longer depending on timeliness of documentation and the complexity of your books.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003eDuring each subsequent month, ongoing Live Bookkeeping services include: an overview of the main features of QBO; setup of customers and vendors; assistance with reports and reporting tools; setup of chart of accounts; assistance with bank connections, expense type classification, categorization, and reconciliation based on information you provide; importing of historical data; and ongoing assistance with bookkeeping practices). Some basic bookkeeping services may not be included and will be determined by your Live Bookkeeper. The Live Bookkeeper will provide help based on the information you provide. For more information about services provided by Live Bookkeeping, refer to the \u003ca href=\"https://glam.app.intuit.com/app/guesttos?glocale=en_US\" data-wa-link=\"disc-qb-tos\" data-action=\"interacted\" data-object=\"content\" data-ui-action=\"clicked\" data-ui-object=\"link\" data-ui-object-detail=\"QuickBooks Terms of Service. \" data-ui-access-point=\"\" data-sku=\"\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" data-object-detail=\"\"\u003eQuickBooks Terms of Service\u003c/a\u003e. \u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cbr\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eQuickBooks Live Bookkeeping Cleanup\u003c/strong\u003e: The QuickBooks Live Bookkeeping Cleanup only applies to bookkeeping records up to your last tax filing. You must have filed your business’ prior tax return and provide a copy of the return before cleanup services can begin. A Live Bookkeeper cannot begin cleaning up your past books until they receive all of the required supporting documentation, which your bookkeeper will request from you after your first meeting. Once your bookkeeper receives all the necessary documentation, they’ll typically complete your cleanup within 30 days. In some cases, your cleanup may take longer depending on timeliness of documentation and the complexity of your books.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cbr\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cbr\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cbr\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eTax-ready books:\u003c/strong\u003e Live Bookkeeping doesn’t include tax preparation services or assistance with tax preparation, or assurance services. Consult a tax preparer for tax advice related to the preparation of your tax return. The Live Bookkeeping Cleanup service is from the date of your last business tax return through the end of the calendar month before first sign-up to Live Bookkeeping.\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003e#Claims\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cbr\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cbr\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan class=\"ql-font-medium01 ql-size-regular\"\u003e1. \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"ql-font-large ql-size-demi\"\u003eTime savings:\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"ql-font-medium01 ql-size-regular\"\u003e Based on a survey of QuickBooks Live Bookkeeping customers, as of November 2021.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cbr\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan class=\"ql-font-medium01 ql-size-regular\"\u003e2. \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"ql-font-large ql-size-demi\"\u003eBookkeeper experience:\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"ql-font-medium01 ql-size-regular\"\u003e Based on internal data, as of November 2021.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cbr\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan class=\"ql-font-medium01 ql-size-regular\"\u003e3. \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"ql-font-large ql-size-demi\"\u003eTax time:\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"ql-font-medium01 ql-size-regular\"\u003e Based on a survey of QuickBooks Live Bookkeeping customers, as of November 2021.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cbr\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan class=\"ql-font-medium01 ql-size-regular\"\u003e4. \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"ql-font-large ql-size-demi\"\u003eMatching:\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"ql-font-medium01 ql-size-regular\"\u003e Customers are automatically matched with a Live Bookkeeper that has experience in their relevant industry, unless one is unavailable. After a customer has connected with the assigned bookkeeper, they may request to be matched with a different bookkeeper, if they prefer.\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cbr\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\u003cp\u003e\u003cspan class=\"ql-font-medium01 ql-size-regular\"\u003e5. \u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan # Quick Start

The easiest way to get started with Dragonfly is with Docker.

## Deployment Method

First, choose a deployment method. 

If you are new to Dragonfly, we recommend the [DragonflyDB Docker Quick Start Guide](/docs/quick-start/)

Other options:

### - [Docker Compose](/contrib/docker/)

### - [Helm Chart for Kubernetes](/contrib/charts/dragonfly/)
